 > 0001 use strict arg arg
 > 0002     if operator("\==", self~StrictDifferent) then return filter
 > 0003     if operator("==", self~StrictEqual) then return filter
 > 0004     if operator("<>", self~CaselessDifferent) then return filter
 > 0005     if operator("=", self~CaselessEqual) then return filter
 > 0006     return self~new(0, arg) -- no operator
 > 0007 
 > 0008     operator: procedure expose arg filter self
 > 0009         use strict arg operatorString, operatorCode
 > 0010         left = arg~left(operatorString~length)
 > 0011         if left~string <> operatorString then return .false
 > 0012         if left~quotedFlags~countStr("1") <> 0 then return .false -- at least one char is quoted
 > 0013         argument = arg~substr(operatorString~length + 1)
 > 0014         filter = self~new(operatorCode, argument)
 > 0015         return .true
